To implement the task, we will create a Python web application using Flask for the backend and React for the frontend. The backend will handle survey management, data analysis, and report generation. The frontend will provide a user interface for capturing surveys and visualizing data.

### Core Classes and Functions:

1. **Backend (Flask)**
   - `app.py`: Main entry point for the Flask application.
     - `create_app()`: Initializes the Flask app and registers blueprints.
   - `routes.py`: Defines API endpoints for survey management.
     - `create_survey()`: Endpoint to create a new survey.
     - `get_surveys()`: Endpoint to retrieve all surveys.
     - `analyze_survey()`: Endpoint to analyze survey data and generate radar charts and heatmaps.
     - `generate_report()`: Endpoint to generate PDF/CSV reports.
   - `models.py`: Defines data models for surveys.
     - `Survey`: Class representing a survey with attributes like title, questions, and responses.
   - `utils.py`: Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
     - `generate_radar_chart()`: Generates a radar chart from survey data.
     - `generate_heatmap()`: Generates a heatmap from survey data.
     - `export_to_pdf()`: Exports data to a PDF report.
     - `export_to_csv()`: Exports data to a CSV file.

2. **Frontend (React)**
   - `App.js`: Main entry point for the React application.
     - `SurveyForm`: Component for capturing survey data.
     - `SurveyList`: Component for displaying a list of surveys.
     - `SurveyAnalysis`: Component for displaying radar charts and heatmaps.

### Backend Implementation

#### app.py

FILENAME: `app.py`

```python
'''

Main entry point for the Flask application.

'''

from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint

def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

#### routes.py

FILENAME: `routes.py`

```python
'''

Defines API endpoints for survey management.

'''

from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv

survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

#### models.py

FILENAME: `models.py`

```python
'''

Defines data models for surveys.

'''

class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

#### App.js

```javascript
'''

Main entry point for the React application.

'''

import React from 'react';
import SurveyForm from './SurveyForm';
import SurveyList from './SurveyList';
import SurveyAnalysis from './SurveyAnalysis';

function App() {
  return (
    <div className="App">
      <h1>Survey Application</h1>
      <SurveyForm />
      <SurveyList />
      <SurveyAnalysis />
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

#### SurveyForm.js

FILENAME: `SurveyForm.js`

```javascript
'''

Component for capturing survey data.

'''

import React, { useState } from 'react';

function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default SurveyForm;
```

#### SurveyList.js

FILENAME: `SurveyList.js`

```javascript
'''

Component for displaying a list of surveys.

'''

import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

function SurveyList() {
  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Logic to fetch surveys from backend
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default SurveyList;
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv

survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv

def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

```js
import React, { useState } from 'react';

function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default SurveyForm;
```

```python
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv

survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv

def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';

function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default SurveyForm;
```

```js
  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default SurveyList;
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Flask application.

from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint
def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

```js
  );
}
```

   ```js
     });
   ```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    // Logic to submit survey data to backend
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

"The highest priority comment is regarding the incomplete implementation of the frontend and backend integration. The React components, such as `SurveyForm` and `SurveyList`, lack the logic to communicate with the Flask backend API endpoints for creating and fetching surveys. This is crucial for the application to function as intended.

**Suggestions on Revision:**

1. **SurveyForm Component:**
   - Implement the logic to submit survey data to the backend API endpoint (`/surveys`).
   - Use `fetch` or `axios` to make a POST request with the survey data.

   ```js
   const handleSubmit = (e) => {
     e.preventDefault();
     fetch('/surveys', {
       method: 'POST',
       headers: {
         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
       },
       body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
     })
     .then(response => response.json())
     .then(data => {
       console.log('Success:', data);
     })
     .catch((error) => {
       console.error('Error:', error);
     });
   };
   ```

2. **SurveyList Component:**
   - Implement the logic to fetch surveys from the backend API endpoint (`/surveys`).
   - Use `fetch` or `axios` to make a GET request and update the `surveys` state.

   ```js
   useEffect(() => {
     fetch('/surveys')
       .then(response => response.json())
       .then(data => setSurveys(data))
       .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching surveys:', error));
   }, []);
   ```

By implementing these changes, the frontend will be able to interact with the backend, allowing users to create and view surveys as required by the task."

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
```

```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv

def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';

function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fetch('/surveys', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default SurveyForm;
```

```js
'''
Component for displaying a list of surveys.
'''
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';

function SurveyList() {
  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/surveys')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => setSurveys(data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching surveys:', error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default SurveyList;
```

 main.py
```python
'''
Main entry point for the Flask application.
'''
from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint

def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv

survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

```js
import React, { useState } from 'react';

function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}

            const newQuestions = [...questions];

      ))}
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Flask application.

from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint
def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

```js
function App() {
  return (
    <div className="App">
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fetch('/surveys', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

surveylist.js
```js
'''
Component for displaying a list of surveys.
'''
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
function SurveyList() {
  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/surveys')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => setSurveys(data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching surveys:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default SurveyList;
```

```python
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    categories = ['Category1', 'Category2', 'Category3']  # Define categories based on survey questions
    values = [response['value'] for response in responses]  # Extract values from responses
    values += values[:1]  # Repeat the first value to close the radar chart

    angles = [n / float(len(categories)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(categories))]
    angles += angles[:1]

    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6), subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))
    plt.xticks(angles[:-1], categories, color='grey', size=8)
    ax.plot(angles, values)
    ax.fill(angles, values, 'b', alpha=0.1)

    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
```

Ensure that the data structure for `responses` is consistent with what the radar chart and heatmap functions expect. Adjust the logic accordingly to fit the actual survey data structure.

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Flask application.
'''
from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint
def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    # Radar chart logic here
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap([[1, 2], [3, 4]], ax=ax)  # Replace with actual data
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fetch('/surveys', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

surveylist.js
```js
'''
Component for displaying a list of surveys.
'''
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
function SurveyList() {
  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/surveys')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => setSurveys(data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching surveys:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default SurveyList;
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv

survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})

@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv

def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    categories = ['Category1', 'Category2', 'Category3']  # Define categories based on survey questions
    values = [response['value'] for response in responses]  # Extract values from responses
    values += values[:1]  # Repeat the first value to close the radar chart

    angles = [n / float(len(categories)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(categories))]
    angles += angles[:1]

    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6), subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))
    plt.xticks(angles[:-1], categories, color='grey', size=8)
    ax.plot(angles, values)
    ax.fill(angles, values, 'b', alpha=0.1)

    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    data = [[response['value'] for response in responses]]  # Replace with actual data structure
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap(data, ax=ax)  # Ensure data is structured correctly
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

```js
import React, { useState } from 'react';

function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fetch('/surveys', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default SurveyForm;
```

'''

```python
class Survey:
    _surveys = []

    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []

    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)

    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys

    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None

    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv

def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    categories = ['Category1', 'Category2', 'Category3']  # Define categories based on survey questions
    values = [response['value'] for response in responses]  # Extract values from responses
    values += values[:1]  # Repeat the first value to close the radar chart

    angles = [n / float(len(categories)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(categories))]
    angles += angles[:1]

    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6), subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))
    plt.xticks(angles[:-1], categories, color='grey', size=8)
    ax.plot(angles, values)
    ax.fill(angles, values, 'b', alpha=0.1)

    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    data = [[response['value'] for response in responses]]  # Replace with actual data structure
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap(data, ax=ax)  # Ensure data is structured correctly
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')

def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Flask application.

from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint
def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    categories = ['Category1', 'Category2', 'Category3']  # Define categories based on survey questions
    values = [response['value'] for response in responses]  # Extract values from responses
    values += values[:1]  # Repeat the first value to close the radar chart
    angles = [n / float(len(categories)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(categories))]
    angles += angles[:1]
    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6), subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))
    plt.xticks(angles[:-1], categories, color='grey', size=8)
    ax.plot(angles, values)
    ax.fill(angles, values, 'b', alpha=0.1)
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    data = [[response['value'] for response in responses]]  # Replace with actual data structure
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap(data, ax=ax)  # Ensure data is structured correctly
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

```js
import SurveyForm from './SurveyForm';
import SurveyList from './SurveyList';
import SurveyAnalysis from './SurveyAnalysis';
function App() {
  return (
    <div className="App">
      <h1>Survey Application</h1>

      <SurveyAnalysis />
    </div>

}
export default App;
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fetch('/surveys', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```

surveylist.js
```js
'''
Component for displaying a list of surveys.
'''
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
function SurveyList() {
  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/surveys')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => setSurveys(data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching surveys:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default SurveyList;
```

```python
Main entry point for the Flask application.

from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint
def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```
models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```
utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    categories = ['Category1', 'Category2', 'Category3']  # Define categories based on survey questions
    values = [response['value'] for response in responses]  # Extract values from responses
    values += values[:1]  # Repeat the first value to close the radar chart
    angles = [n / float(len(categories)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(categories))]
    angles += angles[:1]
    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6), subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))
    plt.xticks(angles[:-1], categories, color='grey', size=8)
    ax.plot(angles, values)
    ax.fill(angles, values, 'b', alpha=0.1)
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    data = [[response['value'] for response in responses]]  # Replace with actual data structure
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap(data, ax=ax)  # Ensure data is structured correctly
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```

```js
'''

import React from 'react';
import SurveyForm from './SurveyForm';
import SurveyList from './SurveyList';
import SurveyAnalysis from './SurveyAnalysis';
function App() {
  return (
    <div className="App">
      <h1>Survey Application</h1>
      <SurveyForm />
      <SurveyList />
      <SurveyAnalysis />
    </div>
  );
}
export default App;
```

surveyform.js
```js
'''
Component for capturing survey data.
'''
import React, { useState } from 'react';
function SurveyForm() {
  const [title, setTitle] = useState('');
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState(['']);
  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fetch('/surveys', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title, questions }),
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
      console.log('Success:', data);
    })
    .catch((error) => {
      console.error('Error:', error);
    });
  };
  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={title}
        onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Survey Title"
      />
      {questions.map((question, index) => (
        <input
          key={index}
          type="text"
          value={question}
          onChange={(e) => {
            const newQuestions = [...questions];
            newQuestions[index] = e.target.value;
            setQuestions(newQuestions);
          }}
          placeholder={`Question ${index + 1}`}
        />
      ))}
      <button type="button" onClick={() => setQuestions([...questions, ''])}>
        Add Question
      </button>
      <button type="submit">Create Survey</button>
    </form>
  );
}
export default SurveyForm;
```
surveylist.js
```js
'''
Component for displaying a list of surveys.
'''
import React, { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
function SurveyList() {
  const [surveys, setSurveys] = useState([]);
  useEffect(() => {
    fetch('/surveys')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => setSurveys(data))
      .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching surveys:', error));
  }, []);
  return (
    <div>
      <h2>Surveys</h2>
      <ul>
        {surveys.map((survey) => (
          <li key={survey.id}>{survey.title}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}
export default SurveyList;
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the Flask application.

from flask import Flask
from routes import survey_blueprint
def create_app():
    app = Flask(__name__)
    app.register_blueprint(survey_blueprint)
    return app
if __name__ == '__main__':
    app = create_app()
    app.run(debug=True)
```

routes.py
```python
'''
Defines API endpoints for survey management.
'''
from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from models import Survey
from utils import generate_radar_chart, generate_heatmap, export_to_pdf, export_to_csv
survey_blueprint = Blueprint('survey', __name__)
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['POST'])
def create_survey():
    data = request.json
    survey = Survey(title=data['title'], questions=data['questions'])
    survey.save()
    return jsonify({'message': 'Survey created successfully'}), 201
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys', methods=['GET'])
def get_surveys():
    surveys = Survey.get_all()
    return jsonify([survey.to_dict() for survey in surveys])
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/analyze', methods=['GET'])
def analyze_survey(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    radar_chart = generate_radar_chart(survey.responses)
    heatmap = generate_heatmap(survey.responses)
    return jsonify({'radar_chart': radar_chart, 'heatmap': heatmap})
@survey_blueprint.route('/surveys/<int:survey_id>/report', methods=['GET'])
def generate_report(survey_id):
    survey = Survey.get_by_id(survey_id)
    pdf_report = export_to_pdf(survey)
    csv_report = export_to_csv(survey)
    return jsonify({'pdf_report': pdf_report, 'csv_report': csv_report})
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines data models for surveys.
'''
class Survey:
    _surveys = []
    def __init__(self, title, questions):
        self.id = len(Survey._surveys) + 1
        self.title = title
        self.questions = questions
        self.responses = []
    def save(self):
        Survey._surveys.append(self)
    @classmethod
    def get_all(cls):
        return cls._surveys
    @classmethod
    def get_by_id(cls, survey_id):
        for survey in cls._surveys:
            if survey.id == survey_id:
                return survey
        return None
    def to_dict(self):
        return {
            'id': self.id,
            'title': self.title,
            'questions': self.questions,
            'responses': self.responses
        }
```

utils.py
```python
'''
Utility functions for data analysis and report generation.
'''
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns
import io
import base64
from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import letter
from reportlab.pdfgen import canvas
import csv
def generate_radar_chart(responses):
    # Example implementation for radar chart generation
    categories = ['Category1', 'Category2', 'Category3']  # Define categories based on survey questions
    values = [response['value'] for response in responses]  # Extract values from responses
    values += values[:1]  # Repeat the first value to close the radar chart
    angles = [n / float(len(categories)) * 2 * 3.14159 for n in range(len(categories))]
    angles += angles[:1]
    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(6, 6), subplot_kw=dict(polar=True))
    plt.xticks(angles[:-1], categories, color='grey', size=8)
    ax.plot(angles, values)
    ax.fill(angles, values, 'b', alpha=0.1)
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def generate_heatmap(responses):
    # Example implementation for heatmap generation
    data = [[response['value'] for response in responses]]  # Replace with actual data structure
    fig, ax = plt.subplots()
    sns.heatmap(data, ax=ax)  # Ensure data is structured correctly
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    plt.savefig(buf, format='png')
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_pdf(survey):
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    c = canvas.Canvas(buf, pagesize=letter)
    c.drawString(100, 750, f"Survey Report: {survey.title}")
    # Add more content to PDF
    c.save()
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.read()).decode('utf-8')
def export_to_csv(survey):
    buf = io.StringIO()
    writer = csv.writer(buf)
    writer.writerow(['Title', 'Questions', 'Responses'])
    writer.writerow([survey.title, survey.questions, survey.responses])
    buf.seek(0)
    return base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue().encode()).decode('utf-8')
```
